No.&#160;333-190335 on Form S-3 (the &#8220;Registration Statement&#8221;) as filed by ALLETE, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) on August 2, 2013, with the Securities and Exchange Commission (&#8220;Commission&#8221;) under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended (&#8220;Securities Act&#8221;), for the registration of an unspecified amount of (a) shares of the Company&#8217;s Common Stock, without par value (&#8220;Common Stock&#8221;) and (b) one or more new series of the Company&#8217;s first mortgage bonds and (2) the Prospectus, dated August 2, 2013 (the &#8220;Prospectus&#8221;), as supplemented by the Prospectus Supplement, dated February 18, 2014 (the &#8220;Prospectus Supplement&#8221;), relating to the sale by the selling shareholder named therein of 396,000 shares (the &#8220;Shares&#8221;) of Common Stock delivered to the selling shareholder by the Company on January 10, 2014.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:16px;text-align:left;text-indent:96px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">I (or attorneys in the Company&#8217;s legal department with whom I have consulted) have participated in the preparation of (a) the Registration Statement, (b) the Prospectus, and (c)&#160;the Prospectus Supplement.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:16px;text-align:left;text-indent:96px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">In furnishing this opinion, I have examined the Amended and Restated Articles of Incorporation, as amended (the &#8220;Charter&#8221;), and the Bylaws, as amended (&#8220;Bylaws&#8221;), of the Company, and have made such further investigation and examined such further documents and records of the Company and certificates of public officials as I have deemed necessary or appropriate for purposes of this opinion.  I have also reviewed all corporate proceedings taken by the Company in respect of the issuance of the Shares.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:16px;text-align:left;text-indent:96px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Based upon the foregoing, I am of the opinion that the Shares are validly issued, fully paid and non-assessable.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:16px;text-align:left;text-indent:96px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">I am a member of the Minnesota Bar and this opinion is limited to the laws of the State of Minnesota and the federal laws of the United States.</font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s0f93674a25b64784a38069e57b908f83"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:16px;text-align:left;text-indent:96px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">I hereby consent to the reference to me in the Prospectus and Prospectus Supplement under the caption &#8220;Legal Opinions&#8221; and to the filing of this opinion as an exhibit to a Current Report on Form 8-K to be filed by the Company on or about February 18, 2014, which will be incorporated by reference in the Registration Statement.  In giving the foregoing consents, I do not thereby admit that I come within the category of persons whose consent is required under Section 7 of the Securities Act or the rules and regulations of the Commission thereunder.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:336px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Sincerely,</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:336px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:336px;font-size:11pt;"><div style="padding-left:0px;text-indent:0px;line-height:normal;padding-top:10px;"><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;width:33.984375%;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;"><tr><td colspan="1"></td></tr><tr><td width="100%"></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:bottom;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">/s/ Deborah A.
